font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On those documents,\nColumbus used a triangular signature of dots and letters that resembled\ninscriptions found on gravestones of Jewish cemeteries in Spain.&nbsp; The Kabbalistic monogram, in Hebrew, Latin,\nand Greek, contains two secret names: Cristobal Colon, his \"nom de\nplume,\" and Salvador Fernando Zarco, Columbus's birth name.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The anagram was a\ncryptic substitute for the Kaddish, a prayer recited in the synagogue by\nmourners after the death of a close relative. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-80HeHeCif0k/UPWNFDa1pDI/AAAAAAAAazs/wGgo44ckIfY/s1600/imagesBHHIK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-80HeHeCif0k/UPWNFDa1pDI/AAAAAAAAazs/wGgo44ckIfY/s1600/imagesBHHIK.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Thus, Columbus's\nsubterfuge allowed his sons to say Kaddish for their crypto-Jewish father when\nhe died.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">At the top left-hand\ncorner of all but one of the 13 letters written by Columbus to his son Diego\ncontained the handwritten Hebrew letters bet-hei, meaning b'ezrat Hashem (with\nGod's help). Observant Jews have for centuries customarily added this blessing\nto their letters. No letters to outsiders bear this mark, and the one letter to\nDiego in which this was omitted was one meant for King Ferdinand.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8p7YfRHcK8o/UPWObABS50I/AAAAAAAAa1M/YSzFK3FnN9k/s1600/Abraham_Parrotman.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"220\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8p7YfRHcK8o/UPWObABS50I/AAAAAAAAa1M/YSzFK3FnN9k/s320/Abraham_Parrotman.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Columbus had a Jew\ninterpreter Luis de Torres on board with him. You always make sure your\ninterpreter can be trusted with your life and that he will NOT describe purple\nas violet. &nbsp;Columbus included de Torres\nbecause de Torres spoke Hebrew. Columbus evidently believed or wanted to\nbelieve that he would meet Hebrew speaking Jews.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-a6JSX2jPyI4/UPWNqfNfoMI/AAAAAAAAa0c/1bfHIo1S8mU/s1600/imagesfghjmk.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"237\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-a6JSX2jPyI4/UPWNqfNfoMI/AAAAAAAAa0c/1bfHIo1S8mU/s400/imagesfghjmk.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When de Torres had landed on\nHispanola he saw a bird which he thought was an Indian peacock and named it \u201ctuki\u201d,\nthe Hebrew word for that bird. &nbsp;Today\nthis bird is called &nbsp;turkey. &nbsp;The indigenous people in South America, the\nCaribbean, and America were named Indians, because Columbus really thought that\nhe was in India and had &nbsp;discovered a\nshort cut to India.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He took six Jews on\nhis voyage, including his interpretor</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;Luis De Torres</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;, Abraham Ben Samuel Zacuto the navigator,&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Mastre Bernal</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;the doctor, Marco the surgeon ,&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">Roderigo Sanchez-inspector</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; and an Isaac Abravanel the astronomer.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LUPGQazdybI/UPWNwYae7ZI/AAAAAAAAa0k/fE-qVob-xqw/s1600/dfgh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"231\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LUPGQazdybI/UPWNwYae7ZI/AAAAAAAAa0k/fE-qVob-xqw/s400/dfgh.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Columbus' diary begins\nwith these words: \u201cIn the same month in which their Majesties issued the edict\nthat all Jews should be driven out of the kingdom and its territories, in the\nsame month, they gave me the order to undertake with sufficient men my\nexpedition of discovery of the Indies.\u201d &nbsp;His voyage began &nbsp;on August 3, 1492.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On March 31, 1492, King\nFerdinand and Queen Isabella proclaimed that all Jews were to be expelled from\nSpain. The edict especially targeted the 80,000 Jews who had never converted,\nand gave them four months to pack up and get out.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-yB5uauwQfEs/UPYtXkwuzVI/AAAAAAAAa30/vZeGUPVMY8M/s1600/imagesnjklo.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-yB5uauwQfEs/UPYtXkwuzVI/AAAAAAAAa30/vZeGUPVMY8M/s1600/imagesnjklo.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Jews were expelled\nfrom Spain on August 2, 1492. Many of these Jews emigrated to Holland, where\nthey set up the Dutch West Indies Company to exploit the new world. In 1654,\nthe first Jew, Jacob Barsimson, emigrated from Holland to New Amsterdam (New\nYork) and in the next decade many more followed him, settling along the East\nCoast, principally in New Amsterdam and Newport, Rhode Island.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UDeG6otOXrk/UPWOChnGRgI/AAAAAAAAa00/WfehlWFMCME/s1600/imagesfgjnm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"301\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UDeG6otOXrk/UPWOChnGRgI/AAAAAAAAa00/WfehlWFMCME/s400/imagesfgjnm.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Columbus started off\nwith deceit. A lookout on the Pinta, Rodrigo de Triana (also known as Juan\nRodr\u00edguez Bermeo), spotted land about 2:00 on the morning of 12 October, and\nimmediately alerted the rest of the crew with a hearty shout. Thereupon, the\ncaptain of the Pinta, Mart\u00edn Alonso Pinz\u00f3n, verified the discovery and alerted\nColumbus by firing a lombard. Columbus later insisted that he was the first to\nsee a light on the land a few hours earlier, &nbsp;( but had kept it within his chest ) thereby\nclaiming for himself the lifetime pension promised by Ferdinand and Isabella to\nthe first person to sight land.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-y2y4qTOUq7s/UPWRljaQtKI/AAAAAAAAa2c/2rYzVGvjfSY/s1600/KOP%5B.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"298\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-y2y4qTOUq7s/UPWRljaQtKI/AAAAAAAAa2c/2rYzVGvjfSY/s400/KOP%5B.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">He raped underage girls\ntoo. In his own words , \"While I was in the boat, I captured a very\nbeautiful Carib woman, whom the said Lord Admiral gave to me. When I had taken\nher to my cabin she was naked - as was their custom. I was filled with a desire\nto take my pleasure with her and attempted to satisfy my desire. She was\nunwilling, and so treated me with her nails that I wished I had never begun.\nBut - to cut a long story short - I then took a piece of rope and whipped her\nsoundly, and she let forth such incredible screams that you would not have\nbelieved your ears. Eventually we came to such terms, I assure you, that you\nwould have thought that she had been brought up in a school for whores--&nbsp;&nbsp; \u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Columbus supervised the\nselling of native girls into sexual slavery. Young girls of the ages 9 to 10\nwere the most desired by his men. In 1500, Columbus casually wrote about it in\nhis log. He said: \"A hundred castellanoes are as easily obtained for a\nwoman as for a farm, and it is very general and there are plenty of dealers who\ngo about looking for girls; those from nine to ten are now in demand.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-JLNDEz548_w/UPWN8Ba6vuI/AAAAAAAAa0s/HGW3KGUSAUw/s1600/imageshk,l.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"214\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-JLNDEz548_w/UPWN8Ba6vuI/AAAAAAAAa0s/HGW3KGUSAUw/s320/imageshk,l.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When he set foot on\nthat sandy beach in the Bahamas on October 12, 1492, Columbus discovered that\nthe islands were inhabited by friendly, peaceful people called the Lucayans,\nTa\u00ednos and Arawaks. Writing in his diary, Columbus said they were a handsome,\nsmart and kind people. He noted that the gentle Arawaks were remarkable for their\nhospitality.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"They offered to share with anyone and when you ask for\nsomething, they never say no,\" he said. The Arawaks had no weapons; their\nsociety had neither criminals, prisons nor prisoners. They were so kind-hearted\nthat Columbus noted in his diary that on the day the Santa Maria was\nshipwrecked, the Arawaks labored for hours to save his crew and cargo. The\nnative people were so honest that not one thing was missing. Columbus was so\nimpressed with the hard work of these gentle islanders, that he immediately\nseized their land for Spain and enslaved them to work in his brutal gold mines.\nWithin only two years, 125,000 (half of the population) of the original natives\non the island were dead.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Df5eF32Dagg/UPWREkhYgYI/AAAAAAAAa2U/w_-h3vHZgWg/s1600/imagesGHUIOO.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Df5eF32Dagg/UPWREkhYgYI/AAAAAAAAa2U/w_-h3vHZgWg/s400/imagesGHUIOO.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Later he made the same\nnice people over 14 years of age deliver a hawk's bell full of gold powder\nevery three months . Once the slaves paid this, they would receive a metal\ntoken. This token was worn around their necks as a signal that they were\nhome-free for another 3 months (during which time they saved up for their next\ntoken, of course.).&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If this tribute was not\ndelivered, they had their hands cut off and were left to bleed to death.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"Gold is a\ntreasure, and he who possesses it does all he wishes to in this world, and\nsucceeds in helping souls into paradise.\" \u2013 Christopher Columbus<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CuC4w19Pu0U/UPWPLQsyHfI/AAAAAAAAa1c/kurtrv57d7U/s1600/GHY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CuC4w19Pu0U/UPWPLQsyHfI/AAAAAAAAa1c/kurtrv57d7U/s400/GHY.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b>During the 2<sup>nd</sup>\nvoyage he took 2 dozen ferocious dogs \u2013 their staple diet was fresh human flesh\ndripping with blood.&nbsp;</b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>Later the dogs became squeamish and would eat only small\nbabies, gnawing their bones with great relish.</b></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Columbus' acts of\ncruelty were so unspeakable and so legendary - even in his own day - that\nGovernor Francisco De Bobadilla arrested Columbus and his two brothers, slapped\nthem into chains, and shipped them off to Spain to answer for their crimes\nagainst the Arawaks. But the King and Queen of Spain, their treasury filling up\nwith gold, pardoned Columbus and let him go free.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XN6ML8BpJac/UPYtcYAZ2XI/AAAAAAAAa38/Pr_jz9IlrFQ/s1600/dfgh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"254\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XN6ML8BpJac/UPYtcYAZ2XI/AAAAAAAAa38/Pr_jz9IlrFQ/s400/dfgh.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">One of Columbus' men,\nBartolome De Las Casas, was so mortified by Columbus' brutal atrocities against\nthe native peoples, that he quit working for Columbus and became a Catholic\npriest. He described how the Spaniards under Columbus' command cut off the legs\nof children who ran from them, to test the sharpness of their blades.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">According\nto De Las Casas, the men made bets as to who, with one sweep of his sword,\ncould cut a person in half. \"Such inhumanities and barbarisms were\ncommitted in my sight as no age can parallel,\" De Las Casas wrote.\n\"My eyes have seen these acts so foreign to human nature that now I\ntremble as I write.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5nYIDAEZpNg/UPWPkPZBfMI/AAAAAAAAa1k/LQ7jeaJ9oqU/s1600/columbus_with-tainos.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5nYIDAEZpNg/UPWPkPZBfMI/AAAAAAAAa1k/LQ7jeaJ9oqU/s400/columbus_with-tainos.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It was a general rule\namong Spaniards to be cruel; not just cruel, but extraordinarily cruel so that\nharsh and bitter treatment would prevent Indians from daring to think of\nthemselves as human beings or having a minute to think at all. So they would\ncut an Indian's hands and leave them dangling by a shred of skin and they would\nsend him on saying \"Go now, spread the news to your chiefs.\"&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">They\nwould test their swords and their manly strength on captured Indians and place\nbets on the slicing off of heads or the cutting of bodies in half with one\nblow. They burned or hanged captured chiefs.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">De Las Casas spent the\nrest of his life trying to protect the helpless native people. But after a\nwhile, there were no more natives to protect. Experts generally agree that\nbefore 1492, the population on the island of Hispaniola probably numbered above\n3 million. Within 20 years of Spanish arrival, it was reduced to only 60,000.\nWithin 50 years, not a single original native inhabitant could be found.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The initial Arawak\npopulation was estimated at 8,000,000. By 1516 only around 12,000 were still\nalive. By 1542, less than 200 remained. By 1555, the Arawaks were all gone.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cRI3FnWUJJM/UPWQf9rUYAI/AAAAAAAAa2E/A5IvFBZCcF4/s1600/imagesJIOP%5B.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cRI3FnWUJJM/UPWQf9rUYAI/AAAAAAAAa2E/A5IvFBZCcF4/s400/imagesJIOP%5B.jpg\" width=\"259\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1498, his five ship\nexpedition brought 1000 Indians to Spain as slaves. . Six hundred of these he\nbrought back to Spain, and the remaining 400 he gave to the Spanish then\n\"governing\" the island.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This was the start of\nthe Trans-Atlantic Enslavement trade, this Atlantic slave trade lasted more\nthan 400 yrs from 1444 to about 1880.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Christopher Columbus derived\nmost of his income from slavery, De Las Casas noted. In fact, Columbus was the\nfirst slave trader in the Americas. As the native slaves died off, they were\nreplaced with black slaves. Columbus' son became the first African slave trader\nin 1505.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Through his exploits in\nHaiti, Columbus lead the way for other European nations to begin seeking wealth\nthrough domination, conquest, and slavery. In essence, Columbus changed the\nworld, and we recognize this in one way or another by delineating history as\nbeing either pre- or post-Columbian.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-DJMyysC5zTA/UPWQ4E6PypI/AAAAAAAAa2M/N6Fv7aQEuwo/s1600/imagesJKKL.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-DJMyysC5zTA/UPWQ4E6PypI/AAAAAAAAa2M/N6Fv7aQEuwo/s400/imagesJKKL.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When Columbus first\nencountered the Caribbean natives, he wrote in his log book of his surprise at\nhow peaceful, naive and seemingly incapable of dishonesty they were. For\nworthless trinkets or sometimes nothing at all, the natives would cheerfully\nhand over whatever possessions were asked for, including gold jewelry. Later,\nanything desired by the Spaniards would simply be taken. Their ignorance of\nweapons such as swords was evident when some natives, while examining Columbus'\nsword, cut themselves on it.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">How unfortunate for the\nnatives that some of them wore gold jewelry when Columbus first landed, and\neven presented him with a few good ones. The sight of this gold inflamed his\ngreed &nbsp;and would soon lead to untold\nsuffering as the natives were forced to work in gold mines.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Columbus wrote:\n\"As soon as I arrived in the Indies, on the first Island which I found, I\ntook some of the natives by force in order that they might learn and might give\nme information of whatever there is in these parts.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The information that\nColumbus wanted most was: Where is the dang gold?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-_IYbwVnGuR8/UPWM-bxUrkI/AAAAAAAAazk/I0WYdpM8nLY/s1600/columbus2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"280\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-_IYbwVnGuR8/UPWM-bxUrkI/AAAAAAAAazk/I0WYdpM8nLY/s400/columbus2.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">One of the few natives\nto actively resist the Spaniards was Hatuey, a Ta\u00edno chief on the island of\nHispaniola. When the Spaniards neared, he fled to Cuba with 400 of his people\nand there carried out a guerilla-style resistance to the Spaniards. After three\nmonths, Hatuey was betrayed and captured and put on a stake to be burned to\ndeath.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before the torch was\napplied, a priest asked Hatney to embrace Christ so that he would go to Heaven.\nHatney asked the priest whether there would be Spaniards in Heaven, to which\nthe priest answered that there were many. Hatuey replied that in that case he\nwould prefer not to go to Heaven, and wanted nothing to do with a God who\nallowed such cruelty as he had witnessed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-eDeqzcoh_EQ/UPYtkP3W4WI/AAAAAAAAa4E/k-ecwOzHpto/s1600/imagesiokjh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"288\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-eDeqzcoh_EQ/UPYtkP3W4WI/AAAAAAAAa4E/k-ecwOzHpto/s320/imagesiokjh.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">An excerpt from\nColumbus\u2019s journal dated 16<sup>th</sup> Dec &nbsp;\u201cThey have no weapons and are all naked\nwithout any skill in arms and are very cowardly so that a thousand would not\nchallenge three,\u201d Thus they are useful to be commanded and to be made to labor\nand sow and to do everything else of which there is need and build towns and be\ntaught to wear clothes and learn our customs.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-NnKMmg-K85I/UPWM4khk5EI/AAAAAAAAazc/4DM1ZKP19fE/s1600/imagesfhj.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">While he is lauded in\nthe United States with a federal holiday and a receives a great deal of credit\nfor discovering North America, his legacy has been tainted by 100% sure ( NOT\nalleged ) charges of genocide , extreme cruelty and heartless\nexploitation.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WTMdzgzNLtY/UPWOJ5vVugI/AAAAAAAAa08/a4Qk5tCsWAU/s1600/imagesGUK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WTMdzgzNLtY/UPWOJ5vVugI/AAAAAAAAa08/a4Qk5tCsWAU/s400/imagesGUK.jpg\" width=\"281\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On the second Monday in\nOctober each year, Americans celebrate Columbus Day . The American children stand in line and sing a nice little song that goes: \"In 1492, Columbus sailed the ocean\nblue.\"&nbsp; It's an all American\ntradition, as American as pizza pie .&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>In fourteen hundred ninety-two<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>Columbus sailed the ocean blue,<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>It was a courageous thing to do<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>But someone was already here.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>Columbus knew the world was round<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>So he looked for the East while westward\nbound,<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>But he didn't find what he thought he\nfound<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>And someone was already here.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>Caribs met him face to face.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>Chorus<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>So tell me, who discover what?<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>He thought he was in a different spot.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><i>Chorus</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The truth is a bit horrible.&nbsp; Columbus is NOT the nice and heroic explorer\nAmericans like to think.. First of all it was Amerigo Vespucci who discovered\nAmerica\u2014NOT Columbus.&nbsp; The Viking, Leif\nEricson&nbsp; founded a Norse village on\nNewfoundland some 500 years earlier.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aYRDAyHtg-U/UPWNdsCP99I/AAAAAAAAa0M/dwc7YtEJ2wY/s1600/imagesxdde.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aYRDAyHtg-U/UPWNdsCP99I/AAAAAAAAa0M/dwc7YtEJ2wY/s1600/imagesxdde.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Native Americans discovered North America\nabout 15 millineums before Columbus was even born! font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Wilden or Versa-matic\ndiaphragm pumps need no special introduction. These are air operated diaphragm\npumps.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-s1R8YxwN7Ik/UPGxOdMtVLI/AAAAAAAAar8/fxgTohqdgHU/s1600/imagesfghhggt4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-s1R8YxwN7Ik/UPGxOdMtVLI/AAAAAAAAar8/fxgTohqdgHU/s1600/imagesfghhggt4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This piece is meant to\nhighlight the safety and chemical resistance aspects. In any case every crew\nmember must be familiar in rigging up a wilden pump as they are used for\nchemical spill contingency.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-7_33IjHPpi4/UPGxSzbyrlI/AAAAAAAAasE/ornIjaUTk44/s1600/imagesfghh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-7_33IjHPpi4/UPGxSzbyrlI/AAAAAAAAasE/ornIjaUTk44/s400/imagesfghh.jpg\" width=\"393\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Wilden pump is not a\nsubmersible pump. You have to keep the pump just above the level of the liquid\nto be pumped.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">There must be an\nawareness of the diaphragm material or the pump is spoilt and worse people\ncould get injured very badly or there could be an explosion. It may develop\nfluid dischg pressure equal to the air supply pressure. Always wear eye\nprotection when working with the pump.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><b><span style=\"color: red;\">See video below to understand how the pump works.</span></b></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/Y6To-bgL4GE/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/Y6To-bgL4GE&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/Y6To-bgL4GE&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On chemical tankers we\ndo not use neoprene or Buna rubber diaphragm wilden pumps. Rather only Teflon\nor Viton pumps are used . SS shell is preferred as many chemicals react with\naluminium and alloys shells.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Usual models supplied on board are M1, M2 and M4\nmodels.&nbsp; An M4 SS model with Teflon\ndiaphragm will weigh about 19 kgs.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Teflon elastomeric\ndiaphragms are not as efficient as rubber as the discharge capacity is reduced\nby 20% and the suction lift is also reduced. The wilden pump in the ballast\npumproom can have a neoprene diaphragm.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If the chemical is\nviscous a larger non collapsible and reinforced inlet pipe is required to avoid\ncavitation. It is critical that on the suction side there must not be any leaks\n. The suction flexible mouth must be sliced off at an angle to mate on to the\ntank bottom. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">M2 pumps are used to mop the couple of litres of condensed water at the Framo deepwell pump suction mouths of all cargo tanks after final steaming.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Drain the compressed\nair line before you use it to power the wilden pump. This is most important if\nyou are using it to pump a water reactive chemical. Imagine heat and exothermic\nsputtering of Sulphuric acid inside the pump because of a leaky diaphragm.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If\nthere are air bubbles in the discharge of the pump it means the diaphragm is\ntorn or the diaphragm plated to pump shaft is not tight.
