font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">It all started on October 21st 1947 at night. Hundreds of\nPathans \u2013 always easy cannon fodder for the Pakistani establishment \u2013 were\ngathered and lined up against the border as the world was in darkness and the\nHindus in Kashmir started their celebrations of Navratri ( 9&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 36px;\">continuous</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;nights of\ncelebrations ). &nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><b><span style=\"color: red;\">THIS HASTY MOVE BY JINNAH WOULD DRIVE KASHMIR INTO THE ARMS OF INDIA FOR EVER --&nbsp;</span></b></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><b><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></b></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><b><span style=\"color: red;\">-- IF BHUTTO WANTED THOUSAND YEARS OF WAR , INDIANS ARE READY TO GIVE ONE MILLION YEARS OF WAR.</span></b><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mahura Power Station was exploded with dynamite and the entire area from border areas with Pakistan to\nall the way near China went into total darkness. &nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">On the other side, the\nMuslim army soldiers in Maharaja Hari Singh\u2019s Army , at Jinnah's instigation, killed their Hindu commander, Col.\nNarain Singh and lit the flares to give the signal to their Pakistani contacts\nand Pathans that all was well and attack could be resumed.</span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hari Singh in distress appealed\nto India for help and acceded to India, when India responded to his cry for\nhelp. Hari Singh signed the Instrument of Accession on October 26, 1947,\nacceding the whole of his princely state (including Jammu, Kashmir, Northern\nAreas, Ladakh, Trans-Karakoram Tract and Aksai Chin) to the Dominion of India.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pakistan\nand India four times went to war against each other and out of which three were\ndue to Kashmir issue. While India holds about 45% of J&amp;K territory and\nPakistan controls 35%, China occupies about 20% which includes Aksai Chin<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Instrument of accession\nexecuted by Maharaja Hari Singh was similar to such instruments executed by the\nrulers of other acceding states. There was no scope for ifs and buts in it.\nAccording to it the signed accession was full, final and irrevocable and not in\nany way conditional or provisional.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Text of letter dated\nOctober 26, J 947 from Sri Hari Singh, the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Maharaja of Jammu and\nKashmir to Lord Mountbatten the GovernorGeneral of India.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>My dear Lord\nMountbatten,<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I have to inform your\nExcellency that a grave emergency has arisen&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">in my State and request\nimmediate assistance of your Government.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As your Excellency is\naware the State of Jammu and Kashmir has&nbsp;</span></i><i style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">not acceded to the\nDominion of India or to Pakistan.&nbsp;</span></i><br />\n<i style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></i>\n<i style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Geographically&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">my State is contiguous\nto both the Dominions. It has vital&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">economical end cultural\nlinks with both of them. Besides my State&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">has a common boundary\nwith the Soviet Republic and China. In&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">their external\nrelations and Dominion of India and Pakistan cannot&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">ignore this fact.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I wanted to take time\nto decide to which Dominion I should accede,&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">or whether it is not in\nthe best interests of both the Dominions and&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">my State to stand\nindependent, of course with friendly and cordial&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">relations with both.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I accordingly\napproached the Dominions of India and Pakistan to&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">enter into Standstill Agreement\nwith my State. The Pakistan&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Government accepted\nthis Agreement. The Dominion of India&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">desired further\ndiscussions with representatives of my Government. l&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">could not arrange this\nin view of the developments indicated below.&nbsp;</span></i><i style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In fact the Pakistan Government\nare operating Post and Telegraph&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">system inside the\nState.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Though we have got a\nStandstill Agreement with the Pakistan&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Government permitted\nsteady and increasing strangulation of&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">supplies like food,\nsalt and petrol to my State.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Afridis, soldiers in\nplain clothes, and desperadoes with modern&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">weapons have been\nallowed to infliter into the State at first in&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Poonch and then in\nSialkot and finally in mass area adjoining&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hazara District on the\nRamkot side.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The result has been that the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">limited number of\ntroops at the disposal of the State had to be&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">dispersed and thus had\nto face the enemy at the several points&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">simultaneously, that it\nhas become difficult to stop the wanton&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">destruction of life and\nproperty and looting.&nbsp;</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Mohara powerhouse which supplies the electric current\nto the whole of Srinagar has&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">been burnt. The number\nof women who have been kidnapped and&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">raped and makes my\nheart bleed. The wild forces thus let loose o&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">the State are marching\non with the aim of capturing Srinagar, the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">summer Capital of my\nGovernment, as first step to over running the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">whole State.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The mass infiltration\ntribesman drawn from the distant areas of the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">North-West Frontier\ncoming regularly in motor trucks using&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mansehra-Muzaffarabad\nRoad and fully armed with up-to-date&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">weapons cannot possibly\nbe done without the knowing of the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Provincial Government\nof the North-West Frontier Province and the&nbsp;</span></i><i style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Government of Pakistan.\nIn spite of repeated requests made by my&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Government no attempt\nhas been made to check these raiders or&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">stop them from coming\nto my State.&nbsp;</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Pakistan Radio even put&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">out a story that a\nProvisional Government has been set up in&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Kashmir. The people of\nmy State both the Muslims generally have&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">North-West Frontier\ncoming regularly in motor trucks using&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mansehra-Muzaffarabad\nRoad and fully armed with up-to-date&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">weapons cannot possibly\nbe done without the knowing of the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Provincial Government\nof the North-West Frontier Province and the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Government of Pakistan.&nbsp;</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In spite of repeated requests made by my&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Government no attempt\nhas been made to check these raiders or&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">stop them from coming\nto my State. The Pakistan Radio even put&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">out a story that a\nProvisional Government has been set up in&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Kashmir. The people of\nmy State both the Muslims generally have&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">taken no part at all.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">With the conditions\nobtaining at present in my State and to great&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">emergency of the\nsituation as it exists, I hay\" no option but to ask&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">for help from the\nIndian Dominion. Naturally they cannot send the&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">help asked for by me\nwithout my State acceding to the Domination&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">of India.&nbsp;</span></i><br />\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></i>\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I have\naccordingly decided to do so and I attach the&nbsp;</span></i><i style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Instrument of Accession\nfor; acceptance by your Government. The&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">other alternative is to\nleave my State and my people to fee-booters.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>On this basis no\ncivilized Government can exist or be maintained.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The alternative I will\nnever allow to happen as long as I am Ruler of&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">the State and I have\nlife to defend my country.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I may also inform your\nExcellency's Government that it is my&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">intention at once to\nset up an interim &nbsp;overnment and ask Shaikh&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Abdullah to carry the\nresponsibilities in this emergency with my&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Prime Minister.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If my State has to be\nsaved immediate assistance must be&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">available at Srinagar.\nMr. VK Krishna Menon is fully aware of the situation and&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">he will explain to you,\nif further explanation is needed.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>In haste and with\nkindest regards.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Yours Sincerely<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Hari Singh<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>The Palace, Jammu<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>26th October, 1947</i><o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zzgYHtMqyAQ/UO_Iy3gefwI/AAAAAAAAafs/qh93F1K56iQ/s1600/imagesyjmm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"283\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zzgYHtMqyAQ/UO_Iy3gefwI/AAAAAAAAafs/qh93F1K56iQ/s400/imagesyjmm.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The Muslim Pathans were&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">in-disciplined</span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;and were NOT briefed properly by Jinnah.&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\">THIS WOULD BE JINNAH'S SECOND AND MORE COSTLY MISTAKE.</b></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b>The Pathans were more\ninterested in rape of attractive women and plunder of wealth.&nbsp;</b></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b><br /></b></span></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b>They made the\nmistake of raping British nuns , even the aged ones, &nbsp;from a monastery --which really pissed off the British. &nbsp;</b></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Major General Douglas\nGracey got the first report of this attack a full two days after it had all\nstarted. &nbsp;Such was the secrecy of Jinnah\u2019s\nplanning. Interestingly, the head of Armies and defense on both sides of the\nborder were British. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Lord Mountbatten was\nhosting a banquet for Thai Foreign Minister. As the guests slowly left the hall\nat the end of the banquet, Indian PM Nehru was requested to stay back and told\nof the first war in Kashmir. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nehru frothed from the mouth talking about the\nUnited Nations, Russia, God Almighty, Edwina\u2019s pull with Rothschild , all and\nsundry until Sardar Patel lost his temper ( as per Mountbatten ) and shouted at\nNehru. \u201cJawaharlal, do you want Kashmir, or do you want to give it away? &nbsp;Give your orders now!\u201d<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-1VFIq8nfziY/UO_vCU3rzpI/AAAAAAAAam0/NT-oUi9wArA/s1600/cvv.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-1VFIq8nfziY/UO_vCU3rzpI/AAAAAAAAam0/NT-oUi9wArA/s1600/cvv.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Seeing Nehru too\nshocked at the outburst, Sardar Patel turned to the Indian army Brigadier Sam\nManeskshaw and cried, \u201cYou have got your dang orders.\u201d <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">By sending Pakistani\nsoldiers dressed up Pathan tribals Jinnah clearly indicted that he does not\naccept an independent Kashmir, which went against him\u2014&nbsp;<b><span style=\"color: blue;\">BIG MISTAKE , JINNAH\nSAAB..&nbsp;</span></b><o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The current indicator supports this-- the so called independent Kashmir out of Northern Territories and \u201cAzad\nKashmir\u201d is usurped and ruled by Pakistan.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Huyo6KCwf7U/UO_QpAZMyeI/AAAAAAAAajs/OGWB6HwlDJU/s1600/hui.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"249\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Huyo6KCwf7U/UO_QpAZMyeI/AAAAAAAAajs/OGWB6HwlDJU/s400/hui.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It was the Sikh\nRegiment under Ranjit Rai that was the first lot to be flown in. By October 27,\nthe Indian troops landed at the Srinagar airport, which had been, until then\ntaken care of by the desh bhakt workers of RSS. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Intriguingly, as soon as Hari Singh signed the\nInstrument of Accession, he was banished from Kashmir by the Indian Government\nand Nehru\u2019s half brother Sheikh Abdullah was put in charge.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hari Singh retired to\nBombay (Mumbai), where he died on 26 April 1961 of a heart attack, aged 65. His\nson Yuvraj (Crown Prince) Karan Singh was appointed 'Sadr-e-Riyasat'\n('President of the Province') in 1952 and Governor of the State in 1964.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Indian forces\nentered Srinagar and quickly reinforced positions. They defeated the Pakistani &nbsp;forces and chased them all the way to &nbsp;Baramulla and Uri. &nbsp;After consolidating Uri and Baramulla with RSS\ncadre , the Indian forces went southwards. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">By that time the Pakistanis\nhad captured Mirpur on November 25, 1947. Then began in Mirpur, followed by\nAlibeg, a large scale massacre of Hindus and Sikhs including indiscriminate raping\nand looting. Around 21,000 people were killed in those massacres and thousands\nof Hindu women raped. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Pakistani forces then\nattacked and captured Jhanger. In Operation Vijay &nbsp;Indian forces recaptured Jhanger and Rajauri.\nThe Pakistani forces meanwhile laid seige on Leh and Kargil. &nbsp;Indian forces took Keran and Gurais. Gilgit\nScouts of Pakistani forces, had major victories in Leh, Skardu and pushed\nfurther into Ladakh.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kP4UOW5ByY0/UO_IooVh3XI/AAAAAAAAafk/8hJqa0s0Q0U/s1600/88.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"148\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kP4UOW5ByY0/UO_IooVh3XI/AAAAAAAAafk/8hJqa0s0Q0U/s400/88.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">At this time, Operation\nDuck \u2013 to attack Dras by the Indians failed. At this time, Indians pushed\nharder and slowly but surely made inroads. &nbsp;Pakistani forces Gilgit forces were over run.\nPoonch, Kargil and Dras were recaptured. &nbsp;Zoji-la Pass was attacked using tanks \u2013 the\nfirst time such war machines were used at that height.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This was the time when\nmessages were sent back to Indian Government by the forces for additional\nammunition and reinforcements. Lord Mountbatten suggested going to UN ( run by\nRothschild ) for a cease fire. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sheikh\nAbdullah, a hard core Islamist at heart who had been put in charge of Kashmir,\nfooled Nehru by suggesting that India could win in plebiscite. &nbsp;He would pay the price as a wiser and furious Nehru would\nincarcerate him later for 17 years.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This set the stage for\nIndia\u2019s going in position of cease-fire, withdrawal of forces and plebiscite\nonce things returned to normal. The UNCIP resolution &nbsp;of August 13, 1948 were adopted by the UN on\nJanuary 5, 1949.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">With this started one\nof the bloodiest and damning chapters of Indian sub-continent.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-CbuTctTn7-4/UO_QhmqzPAI/AAAAAAAAajk/7b7xPCGDYlU/s1600/imagesvgtuio.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-CbuTctTn7-4/UO_QhmqzPAI/AAAAAAAAajk/7b7xPCGDYlU/s400/imagesvgtuio.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>Kashmir cannot claim\nself-determination. Indians are NOT stupid. &nbsp;Kashmir's accession is final and irrevocable as there is in law\nno such thing as a provisional accession. &nbsp;</b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">After the demographics\nof Kashmir have changed by Islamic terrorism , (Kashmir is now estimated to be\n64% Muslim.), we are not stupid to hold a referendum now. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Plebiscite could not be held at the right time,\n</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">because of Pakistan's non-cooperation. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">In 1953 elected members of the Jammu &amp;\nKashmir state assembly ratified Kashmir accession to India.</span></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b>&nbsp;</b></span><br /><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">India didn't sign any\nbinding agreement to hold a plebiscite. This UN resolution is not\nenforcable.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Yes Nehru under Edwina\u2019s\ninfluence may have verbally promised a plebiscite --but he also&nbsp; made hundreds of other verbal promises.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-81TL-4lSJKM/UO_J4oyxsZI/AAAAAAAAahE/o3gzpEboZw4/s1600/imagesjyui.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-81TL-4lSJKM/UO_J4oyxsZI/AAAAAAAAahE/o3gzpEboZw4/s400/imagesjyui.jpg\" width=\"339\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">So what\u2019s\nthe big deal ?&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">The point&nbsp; is India didn't sign any written agreement to\nhold plebiscite. Whereas Pakistan signed an agreement (Shimla) to resolve of\nall pending issues including Kashmir bilaterally.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">This agreement was signed\nafter UN resolution. So Shimla agreement takes precedence over any UN\nresolution.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">End of story.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\"><b>TOUGH LUCK PAKISTAN !</b></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\"><b><br /></b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-s1LWR3prQ34/UO_QbJmkHHI/AAAAAAAAajc/lv-wryPwngU/s1600/imagesghui.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-s1LWR3prQ34/UO_QbJmkHHI/AAAAAAAAajc/lv-wryPwngU/s400/imagesghui.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Between 15th August\n1947 and 26 th October 1947, &nbsp;Hari Singh lost\n1/3 of Kashmir to invaders unleashed by Jinnah.&nbsp;\nOn 26th October 1947 Hari Singh was on the verge of losing his capital\nSrinagar, that is when he decided to seek Indian help and joined India. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: large;\"><b>Haste makes waste, Jinnah saab!</b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As Nehru and VK Krisha Menon argued at UN in\n1948,&nbsp; because India has a signed\ndocument that states Kashmir belongs to India, all Pakistani claims and actions\nin the region are null and void . Any aggression demonstrating a blatant\ndisregard to international law and procedure would be given a moonh tod jawab .</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Even before Article 370\nwas gifted to Sheikh Abdullah\u2019s Kashmir, strange provisions like having a\nseparate Constitution for Kashmir (as opposed to Indian Constitution), use of\nNational Conference flag (as opposed to Indian tricolor), and special permit\nfor Indians to visit Kashmir has been in place. Article 370 merely formalized\nthese and more.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dictator Sheikh\nAbdullah ran a brutal police raj where Hindus were always at the receiving end. &nbsp;Kashmiri\nPandit &nbsp;Premnath Dogra launched Praja\nParishad, a democratic outfit to challenge the \u201cpartial to Muslims\u201d activities\nof Abdullah. &nbsp;For 3 years, as they\nagitated and were brutally crushed by Abdullah\u2019s police, while the Indian\nGovernment under Nehru remained quiet. This was the first taste of future\nbrutalities the Kashmiri Pandits would suffer .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Only Dr. Shyama Prasad\nMookherjee who was Minister for Industry and Supply in Prime Minister\nJawaharlal Nehru's cabinet rose up to the plight of Kashmiri Pandits and\nmarched to Kashmir. As he reached Jammu\u2019s border on 11<sup>th</sup> May 1953, ,\nhe was arrested by Sheikh Abdullah\u2019s special police and thrown into Srinagar\njail. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EhEzDeV_nOU/UO-n9NoU7UI/AAAAAAAAaZk/DPPJ25hDnUE/s1600/hhh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EhEzDeV_nOU/UO-n9NoU7UI/AAAAAAAAaZk/DPPJ25hDnUE/s320/hhh.jpg\" width=\"242\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">His Bharatiya Jana Sangh comrade Atal\nBiharee Vajpaye saw him being led away by Sheikh Abdullah\u2019s police.&nbsp; Mukherjee turned back looked into Vajpaye\u2019s\neyes and cried \u201c Do not give up the struggle\u201d . &nbsp;This was the last time he would be seen . &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">He was murdered in jail by a Penicillin injection\non 23<sup>rd</sup> June 1953 for a dry pleurisy , though he kept pleading loudly\nthat he is allergic to Penicillin.&nbsp; This\nwas Abdullah\u2019s way of revenge . But within 5 weeks there would be most severe retribution.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">For on 11 February 1941 S P Mookerjee told a\nHindu rally that if Muslims wanted to live in Pakistan they should \"pack\ntheir bag and baggage and leave India... (to) wherever they like\".&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The\nMuslims had not forgotten the help given by sister group RSS to Indian soldiers who drove\naway the Pakistani Pathan tribesmen.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Both he and his &nbsp;father was Sir Ashutosh Mukherjee, were Vice-Chancellors\nof the University of Calcutta. At the age of 33, he became the youngest\nVice-Chancellor of the University of Calcutta (1934), and held the office till\n1938.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dr.Syama Prasad\nMookerjee opposed the Indian National Congress's decision to grant Kashmir a\nspecial status with its own flag and Prime Minister. According to Congress's\ndecision, no one, including the President of India could enter into Kashmir\nwithout the permission of Kashmir's Prime Minister.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; His mother Lady Jogmaya Devi requested\nthe setting up of an impartial enquiry. Nehru however ignored the letter and no\nenquiry commission was set up. &nbsp;Mookerjee's\ndeath therefore remains a matter of great controversy. &nbsp;Atal Bihari Vajpayee claimed in 2004 that the\ndeath of Mookherjee was a \"Nehru conspiracy\".<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Meanwhile, the member\nof the Indian Constituent Assembly. Handoo,\nand Maulana Abul Kalam Azad all in turn,&nbsp;\ngave detailed proof of what Sheikh Abdullah was up to \u2013 and his DOUBLE\nAGENT agenda.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Pakistani &nbsp;conspiracy of the Sheikh was submitted to Nehru along with documentary\nevidence and recorded tapes of his secret and public speeches. Nehru\nwas taken aback while listening to the tapes and going through the handwritten letters\nof Sheikh Abdullah.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Also the hue and cry\nfrom the Indian masses suddenly changed the scenario . Nehru was now skating on\nthin ice and he would have been deposed if he continued protecting his alleged Muslim half\nbrother.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In May 1946 Sheikh\nAbdullah launched the Quit Kashmir agitation against the Maharajah Hari Singh\nand was arrested and sentenced to three years imprisonment but was released\nonly sixteen months later on 29 September 1947. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">His cabinet\nminister Bakshi Ghulam Mohammed was appointed as Prime Minister. Sheikh Abdullah\nwas immediately arrested and later jailed for eleven years.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Abdullah along with\nMirza Afzal Beg and 22 others were accused of conspiracy against the Indian state\n</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">for espousing the seditious cause of an\nindependent Kashmir.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On 8 April 1964 the State Government dropped\nall charges &nbsp;and Sheikh Abdullah was\nreleased and returned to Srinagar where he was accorded a great welcome by the Muslims\nof the valley as&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Sher-e-Kashmir (the Lion of Kashmir)</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nehru was suffering from a secret brain disease and he would die\nwithin 3 weeks. &nbsp;Nehru reconciled with Abdullah before his death, for his daughter Indira's sake.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Muslims in India do NOT want to settle down in Pakistan. , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The Constitution can be amended only by the Parliament as per procedure clearly laid out in Article 368. but Article 35A was never presented before the Parliament of India\u2026</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; My book is nothing but a simple historic record of facts. I shall place before the reader the theories of the Hindus exactly as they are, and I shall mention in connection with them similar theories of the Greeks in order to show the relationship existing between them.(1910, Vol. 1, p. 7;1958, p. 5)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Hindus considered Muslims violent and impure, and did not want to share anything with him.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Over time, Al-Biruni won the welcome of Hindu scholars. Al-Biruni collected books and studied with these Hindu scholars to become fluent in Sanskrit, discover and translate into Arabic the mathematics, science, medicine, astronomy and other fields of arts as practiced in 11th century India. He was inspired by the arguments offered by Indian scholars who believed earth must be ellipsoid shape, with yet to be discovered continent at earth's south pole, and earth's rotation around the sun is the only way to fully explain the difference in daylight hours by latitude, seasons and earth's relative positions with moon and stars.[36] Al-Biruni was also critical of Indian scribes who he believed carelessly corrupted Indian documents while making copies of older documents.[37] Al-Biruni's translations as well as his own original contributions reached Europe in 12th and 13th century, where they were actively sought.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">CONTINUED TO 2--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">CONTINUED FROM 1--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">While others were killing each other over religious differences, Al-Biruni had a remarkable ability to engage Hindus in peaceful dialogue. Mohammad Yasin puts this dramatically when he says, \u201cThe Indica is like a magic island of quiet, impartial research in the midst of a world of clashing swords, burning towns, and burned temples.\u201d (Indica is another name for Al-Biruni\u2019s history of India). Algorism and algorithm stem from Algoritmi, the Latin form of his name.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Let me quote wikipedia:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">QUOTE- Ibn al-Nad\u012bm's Kit\u0101b al-Fihrist includes a short biography on al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b together with a list of the books he wrote. Al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b accomplished most of his work in the period between 813 and 833. After the Muslim conquest of Persia, Baghdad became the centre of scientific studies and trade, and many merchants and scientists from as far as China and India traveled to this city, as did al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b. He worked in Baghdad as a scholar at the House of Wisdom established by Caliph al-Ma\u2019m\u016bn, where he studied the sciences and mathematics, which included the translation of Greek and Sanskrit scientific manuscripts.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b's Z\u012bj al-Sindhind[11] (Arabic: \u0632\u064a\u062c \u0627\u0644\u0633\u0646\u062f \u0647\u0646\u062f\u200e, \"astronomical tables of Sindh and Hind\") is a work consisting of approximately 37 chapters on calendrical and astronomical calculations and 116 tables with calendrical, astronomical and astrological data, as well as a table of sine values. This is the first of many Arabic Zijes based on the Indian astronomical methods known as the sindhind.[22] The work contains tables for the movements of the sun, the moon and the five planets known at the time. This work marked the turning point in Islamic astronomy. Hitherto, Muslim astronomers had adopted a primarily research approach to the field, translating works of others and learning already discovered knowledge.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; Then he would go ahead until he reached the level ground where he would stand facing the qiblah, and he stood for a long time, offering du\u2019aa\u2019 and raising his hands. These people are survivors in the original\nsense.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">They are intense people\nand totally dedicated to their purpose. Their ability to focus on a&nbsp; creative project is awesome. They are usually\nextremists with extreme tempers and always have an under current of uneasiness\nwithin them.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When it comes to passion,\nfeelings can get out of perspective because emotional reactions can swamp and\noverwhelm reasoning. Such people must marry docile and understanding women.\nPeople with this line can find some aspects of relating to others problematic.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">They will not easily adhere to the usual norms of society.&nbsp;&nbsp; In extreme cases, they will be completely\nruled by passions and instincts and the law of the jungle will apply, hence the\nname given to the line. They tend to think in absolutes and to be very focused\non what interests them to the exclusion of other important factors.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-BSXQIFYFsD4/UOwFbSG9XmI/AAAAAAAAaWs/t7tVhOaZTRA/s1600/simianmirror.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"200\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-BSXQIFYFsD4/UOwFbSG9XmI/AAAAAAAAaWs/t7tVhOaZTRA/s200/simianmirror.jpg\" width=\"148\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Simian line\npeople find it difficult to lead a&nbsp;\nbalanced life.&nbsp; They focus\nentirely on either their work or their relationship, or on something else in a\nlop sided manner. They hold on to old resentments and then explode in a tantrum\nor floods of tears.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Such people can be very obstinate. They tend to be emotionally\nand psychologically closed people, socially awkward, with one-track minds .&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; THE AYURVEDIC DOCTOR HAD DIFFERENT METHODS..<br /><br />The Shiva Swarodaya advises that for good health the sadhaka and yogi should maximize the flow of ida during the day and the flow of pingala at night. ..<br /><br />If there is too much heat in the body, lying on the right side can help cool it. .<br /><br />Conversely when the body is excessively cold, lying on the left side can help to warm it. .<br /><br />YOU CAN WATCH SENPAKU DISAPPEAR BY BLOCKING THE APPROPRIATE NOSTRIL WITH A COTTON PLUG..<br /><br />The state of our body and mind is reflected in the alternation of the swara cycles. If either nadi predominates for too long, it is a sign or warning that one of the branches of the autonomic nervous system is being overstressed and only one of the brain hemispheres is being fully utilized.<br /><br />If ida flows for a long time beyond the normal schedule, this signifies some imbalance in the mind. Or if pingala flows beyond schedule, there is some sort of imbalance in the pranic body.<br /><br />When the physical and mental energies are unbalanced, the personality is only half developed .<br /><br />SENPAKU EYED STUDENTS ARE NOT ADMITTED IN KALARI CLASSES . HE IS TOLD TO DO INTENSE NADI SHODANA PRANAYAMA AND SURYA NAMSASKAR TO EASE HIS SENPAKU.<br /><br />Prapanchasara Tantra talks about AGNI ( tattwa ) affecting the eyes ..<br /><br />The first tattwa which manifested was akasha or ether, so-called because of its subtle, all-pervading and motionless nature. From ether came vayu or air, which is prana in a subtle state, but there is movement, something like the nature of the wind. From vayu, agni (fire) evolved, where prana became hot like fire. As it cooled it became apas (water) and could flow like a stream of water.<br /><br />When it settled, it became immovable, like a rock, prithvi or the earth. In this way the nature of the tattwas indicates the influence and effect of prana when it operates at these particular frequencies.<br /><br />In astrology the elements represent particular levels of vibration and influence at the cosmic level. In swara yoga these elements and vibrations<br />are seen to be present within the individual structure.<br /><br />So we do not have to look into the universe because the macrocosm is mirrored in the microcosm.<br /><br />CONTINUED TO 2--</div>\n<span class=\"comment-actions secondary-text\" id=\"bc_0_74MN\" kind=\"m\"><span class=\"item-control blog-admin pid-1783552029\" style=\"display: inline;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_74BR\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replybox-single\" id=\"bc_0_74B_box\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; margin-top: 5px;\">\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_75B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c2278763322455477534\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_75M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. These tattwas are indicative of sychophysiological states and cause the breath to flow in different directions on exhalation.<br /><br />If you know which tattwa is active, you can judge your physical, mental and emotional state and gauge it according to whatever task you are about to undertake. But more than this, the practice increases our mundane<br /><br />awareness and experience so that a deeper understanding grows of who and what we are. Tattwas are not physical and chemical elements. They refer to a particular level of energy, sound frequency and light emanation.<br /><br />FATE RULES PREDOMINANT IN A SEMPAKU -- HE IS UNABLE TO FORGE THE HINGES OF HIS DESTINY ON HIS OWN TERMS<br /><br />Before the actual onset of a disease, the flow of the swara becomes disturbed, and if this is noted beforehand, then the imbalance can be rectified and the sickness averted.
