, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">She also became the traveling\ncompanion of a wealthy heiress who had a library of hundreds of ancient Indian\nbooks that she always took with her. This is no doubt where Blavatsky got much\nof her material to plagiarize from.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In India she became more spiritual enrolled the services of&nbsp; Damodar K\nMavalankar to be her side kick for her seance shrine room magic tricks to\nbamboozle all. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1879 Damodar met\nHenry Steel Olcott and H. P. Blavatsky in Bombay, after they had just\nestablished the Theosophical Society's temporary Indian headquarters there. &nbsp;Damodar joined the Society and his Maharastrian\nBrahmin family ex-communicated him . He promptly went to Sri Lanka and\nbecame a Buddhist along with Henry Steel Olcott and H. P. Blavatsky.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">His family\ncut him off from the will as he could NOT marry the Brahmin girl who was betrothed\nto him in his childhood. In response to this, Damodar gave up an income of\n50,000 Indian rupees ( a large amount those days ) to provide for the future of\nhis wife, &nbsp;and continued to live and work\nwith Blavastky. He continued his work in this way until 1885, when Blavatsky\nleft India and then he went to Tibet.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EhDT6E00T08/UNrNalHFFEI/AAAAAAAAaM4/ezk5s8L0NhQ/s1600/imagesDKM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EhDT6E00T08/UNrNalHFFEI/AAAAAAAAaM4/ezk5s8L0NhQ/s400/imagesDKM.jpg\" width=\"313\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Blavatsky used Damodar\nand a certain Mr and Mrs Coloumb to prop her up as a super magician nay Messiah\nwith divine powers.&nbsp; Finally in 1885 it was Mr Alexis.\nand Mrs. Emma Coulomb who ratted on her, revealing all the trap-door tricks of her\nside-show Mahatmas and her \u201capparitions.\u201d-- forcing her to flee from India for ever on March 31st 1885. &nbsp;They admitted that they were side kicks like Damodar.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Osho himself said &nbsp;QUOTE <i>&nbsp;While\nshe was traveling by train she would be in first class and Damodar would be in\nthird class. Suddenly Damodar would fall flat on the floor of the compartment,\nunconscious, foaming. Naturally, the train was stopped, people gathered and\nthen Madame Blavatsky would come and do some abracadabra. Damodar would\nimmediately open his eyes and everybody would see \u2013\u201cwhat a tremendously\nspiritual powerful woman\u201d... And nobody knew that he was her side kick &nbsp;and that was his only job</i>. UNQUOTE<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Richard Hodgson, a\nmember of&nbsp; the Society for Psychical\nResearch (London)&nbsp; arrived in India to\ninquire into and report on the Coulombs\u2019 allegations. Based upon Hodgson\u2019s\nfindings, the S.P.R. committee in its final report of December, 1885, branded\nMadame Blavatsky \"one of the most accomplished, ingenious and interesting\nimpostors in history.</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Blavatsky had ordered\nMr. Alexis Coulomb to cut a secret hole in the ceiling for receipt of Mahatma\nLetters. The shrine in the occult Room was fitted with a secret back door. In\nfact, the whole occult Room was rigged with all manners of tricks which Emma\nknew, being part of it. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">There was a hidden\nhole in back of the shrine from whence all manner of spirit manifestations\ncould be manipulated. &nbsp;The ex-confederate\ncouple , the Coulombs hijacked by the Catholic church, also revealed Blavatsky\nhad secret passages and hidden doors built into her house which aided her in\ndeceiving people about her \"psychic abilities\". &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Blavatsky dubbed\nherself a 'Priestess of Isis', and combined Spiritualism, Cabala, Western\noccultism, Hinduism and Buddhism along with a dash of Darwinian evolution, to\nmake the whole thing sound 'scientific'\u2014and the world cried WOW!.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">A German occultist\nrevival began in 1884 with the foundation of the German section of the\nTheosophical Society under the presidency of Dr. Wilhelm H\u00fcbbe-Schleiden.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Toward the last days of\nher life Blavatsky wrote a confession to one of her detractors, a Russian\nwriter named Solyvov, and admitted she had lied about many things, including\nthe existence of the Mahatmas, &nbsp;her faked\ncommunications with spirits and her psychic powers . The letter was written in\nan &nbsp;most dramatic manner possible, making\nherself sound like a persecuted martyr ( for Big Brother ) rather than a fraud. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Though Blavatsky was\nproven a fraud in her lifetime and even finally admitted it, her Theosophical\nSociety continues on. There are chapters in several countries even today,\nincluding the U.S and her HQ at Adyar in India .&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Her followers will even say\nthings like \"Sure, Blavatsky had a streak of charlatanism in her, &nbsp;but you have to look past that and read her\nteachings for what they really are.\"&nbsp;\n&nbsp;She was good in sifting through\nIndian wisdom and weaving it together in a shoddy manner\u2014even then it was good\nenough for the West. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Probably it struck a\nchord for she was the first to introduce the Hindu concept of reincarnation\ninto Western spiritualism\u2014and she ran down Jesus Christ and Christianity with\nall their Inquisitions. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lMwJJJpzIRE/UNrbhSXDRiI/AAAAAAAAaOE/Gcj4ZekVsdc/s1600/images+(1).jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lMwJJJpzIRE/UNrbhSXDRiI/AAAAAAAAaOE/Gcj4ZekVsdc/s320/images+(1).jpg\" width=\"301\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">She produced two\namazing society members , both Indians. &nbsp;The\nfirst was<span style=\"color: red;\"><b> Jiddu Krishnamurthy</b></span> who WOWED the west with his amazing and astounding intellect\nand the other was UG Krishnamurthy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>A Spiritual &nbsp;order was formed by Theosphists called The\nOrder of The Star in The East to introduce Jiddu Krishnamurty as the new 'World\nTeacher', for which he was more than qualified.&nbsp;&nbsp;</i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>But in 1929 Jiddu Krishnamurti dissolved the order during an address he\ngave before the group in 1929, which shocked and angered them. &nbsp;</i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Theosophist leaders had unwittingly set\nthemselves up for such a thing to happen, having told their gullible followers\nover the years that the 'World Teacher' might someday say things that were\ncompletely unexpected and contrary to their preconceived notions, and it would\nbe unwise and even 'dangerous' not to do as he instructed! &nbsp;</i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Ironically, Krishnamurti is now known as the\n'un-guru', because he told seekers that they should forgo all religions and all\ngurus (including Theosophy) and try to find answers themselves.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">An 1892 periodical,\nLotus Blossoms, featured Blavatsky's writings and \"was the first German\npublication to sport the theosophical swastika upon its cover\". Many\nGerman occultists who read Blavatsky's works loved the idea about being\nracially superior to the rest of humanity, and wrote books of their own\npromoting the idea as early as the 19th Century. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1902 Dr. Rudolph\nSteiner became Secretary-General of the German section of the Theosophical\nSociety. In 1912, he and a group of his followers broke away from the Theosophical Society and\nfounded the Anthroposophical Society. &nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">German Rudolf Steiner left, in protest, as he could NOT swallow the idea of Annie\nBesant promoting brown skinned Jiddu Krishnamurthy being the new messiah. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Building\non Theosophy's doctrine of root races, Steiner further built on the myth of\nAryan supremacy, saying Aryans were more \"spiritually advanced\" than\nthe other races and that their time had arrived. The similarities with many of\nSteiner's bizarre doctrines and Nazi ideas are unmistakable.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nazi occultists\nbelieved ancient German tribes were the true keepers of the Ancient Mysteries\nwhich had their origin in Atlantis, when seven races of God-men were introduced\nto Earth</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This\n\"S.P.R.-Hodgson\" Report did her in--yet she continued as a writer,\nfilling up her books with plagiarized Indian Vedic stuff. .&nbsp; She wrote two occult best sellers, Isis\nUnveiled (1887)&nbsp; and&nbsp; The Secret Doctrine (1888), which are still\nin print.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">During 1889 Blavatsky finished\ntwo more books before her death .-- The Key to Theosophy an introduction to theosophical thought\nand philosophy, and The Voice of the Silence, a mystical and poetic work on the\npath of enlightenment.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-wU662Lb15fU/UNs6SqrgZ_I/AAAAAAAAaPQ/oLAIylTDIAk/s1600/Madame+Blavatsky_London_1884.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"276\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-wU662Lb15fU/UNs6SqrgZ_I/AAAAAAAAaPQ/oLAIylTDIAk/s320/Madame+Blavatsky_London_1884.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In July, 1890, Madame\nBlavatsky established the European Headquarters of the Theosophical Society at\n19 Avenue Road, St. John\u2019s Wood, London. From this address H.P. Blavatsky died\non May 8, 1891, during a severe epidemic of flu in England, and her remains\nwere cremated at Woking Crematorium, Surrey.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Part of her ashes were scattered in India.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Theosophical\nSociety is open today to anybody who supports its three objectives, regardless\nof belief, social custom or marriage status. &nbsp;Celibacy is neither encouraged nor\ndiscouraged, each member being free to decide his own way of life. General\nphilosophical outlook , universal brotherhood, belief in theory of Karma and reincarnation\n. Nothing is mandatory. Members are free to have any or no spiritual practice\nat all.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Blavatsky made Vatican her No 1 enemy when she wrote &nbsp;\u201cThe Christians\nand scientists must be made to respect their Indian betters. This is NOT a dance of opposites. In Hinduism we call the MALE- purusha and FEMALE- prakriti.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, freeserif, serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, freeserif, serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">In the Tantric cosmology, the whole universe is perceived as being created, penetrated and sustained by two fundamental forces, which are permanently in a perfect, indestructible UNION. These forces or universal aspects are called Shiva ( Purusha ) and Shakti (Prakriti ).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, freeserif, serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, freeserif, serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">Each of the trinity gods are powerless without their consorts.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, freeserif, serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, freeserif, serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">Purusha and Pragati is expressed as Shiva and Shakti in the same body 50:50 \u2013 this is NOT a she boy or a transgender . It is a mindboggling, intelligent concept.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, freeserif, serif; font-size: 16px; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Akshaya Patra started off as a Non-Governmental\nOrganization in India which free meals to underprivileged children.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-g11r5s1KNLw/UNPyoS3px0I/AAAAAAAAZ7M/jx5tgkJZX1E/s1600/ghy.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; line-height: 150%;\">At this, Dhaumya, the priest of the Pandavas,\ncounselled him to pray to Lord Surya. Pleased with Yudhishtira's prayers, Lord\nSurya blessed him with the Akshaya Patra, a vessel that would give unlimited\nfood every day till Draupadi who ate last , finished eating.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FHIUl06gHkY/UNPyujxgHiI/AAAAAAAAZ7U/DUZdqYlVFgo/s1600/images+(3).jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FHIUl06gHkY/UNPyujxgHiI/AAAAAAAAZ7U/DUZdqYlVFgo/s320/images+(3).jpg\" height=\"224\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In June 2000, ISKON started\na proper mid-day meal program in Bangalore called Akshaya Patra by feeding 1500\nchildren in 5 schools. &nbsp;At that time\nthere was no state run school meal program in Karnataka. &nbsp;This programme attracted street urchins to\nstudy in schools which provided free food. It was noted that these poor\nchildren did well in academics and they beat the rich privileged kids in merit.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This prompted the\nSupreme Court of India to pass an order on November 28, 2001 that \u201cCooked\nmid-day meal is to be provided in all the government and government-aided\nprimary schools in all the states.\u201d &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-N7btJrc2UZ4/UNN0OUtjdyI/AAAAAAAAZzg/4oLvdIrdTJQ/s1600/downloadgioo.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-N7btJrc2UZ4/UNN0OUtjdyI/AAAAAAAAZzg/4oLvdIrdTJQ/s1600/downloadgioo.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Akshaya\nPatra was called in to give testimonies to the Supreme Court in order to\nimplement the mandate. &nbsp;The Akshaya Patra\nFoundation (TAPF) is a public, charitable, secular Trust, registered in\nBangalore. The Board of Trustees comprise missionaries of ISKCON Bangalore,\ncorporate professionals, and entrepreneurs.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">More children joined\nschool from desperately poor families just to have one proper square meal a day\nwhich their parents could not afford.&nbsp; More\nthan 14 million underprivileged children in India are out of school and into\nchild labor in order to earn a single meal in a day. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;
